Local Open Scope cat.

(** ** Definitions *)

(** A precategory is a pregroupoid when all of its arrows are [iso]s. *)
Definition is_pregroupoid (C : category) :=
  ∏ (x y : C) (f : x --> y), is_z_isomorphism f.


C: category
isaprop (is_pregroupoid C)


C: category
isaprop (is_pregroupoid C)

  
C: category
t, t0: C
t1: C ⟦ t, t0 ⟧
isofhlevel 1 (is_z_isomorphism t1)

  apply isaprop_is_z_isomorphism.
Defined.

Definition pregroupoid : UU := ∑ C : category, is_pregroupoid C.

(** Constructors, accessors, and coersions *)
Definition make_pregroupoid (C : category) (is : is_pregroupoid C) : pregroupoid :=
  (C,, is).
Definition pregroupoid_to_precategory : pregroupoid -> category := pr1.
Definition pregroupoid_is_pregroupoid :
  ∏ gpd : pregroupoid, is_pregroupoid (pr1 gpd) := pr2.
Coercion pregroupoid_to_precategory : pregroupoid >-> category.

(** A category is a groupoid when all of its arrows are [iso]s. *)
Definition groupoid : UU := ∑ C : category, is_pregroupoid C.

(** Constructors, accessors, and coersions *)
Definition make_groupoid (C : category) (is : is_pregroupoid C) : groupoid := (C,, is).
Definition groupoid_to_category : groupoid -> category := pr1.
Definition groupoid_is_pregroupoid :
  ∏ gpd : groupoid, is_pregroupoid (pr1 gpd) := pr2.
Coercion groupoid_to_category : groupoid >-> category.
Definition groupoid_to_pregroupoid :
  groupoid → pregroupoid := λ gpd, make_pregroupoid gpd (groupoid_is_pregroupoid gpd).
Coercion groupoid_to_pregroupoid : groupoid >-> pregroupoid.

Definition univalent_groupoid : UU := ∑ C : univalent_category, is_pregroupoid C.

(** Constructors, accessors, and coersions *)
Definition make_univalent_groupoid (C : univalent_category) (is : is_pregroupoid C) :
  univalent_groupoid := (C,, is).
Definition univalent_groupoid_to_univalent_category :
  univalent_groupoid -> univalent_category := pr1.
Coercion univalent_groupoid_to_univalent_category :
  univalent_groupoid >-> univalent_category.
Definition univalent_groupoid_is_pregroupoid :
  ∏ ugpd : univalent_groupoid, is_pregroupoid (pr1 ugpd) := pr2.
Definition univalent_groupoid_to_groupoid :
  univalent_groupoid -> groupoid :=
  λ ugpd, make_groupoid ugpd (univalent_groupoid_is_pregroupoid ugpd).
Coercion univalent_groupoid_to_groupoid :
  univalent_groupoid >-> groupoid.

(** An alternative characterization of univalence for groupoids *)
Definition is_univalent_pregroupoid (pgpd : pregroupoid) :=
  (∏ a b : ob pgpd, isweq (fun path : a = b => idtomor a b path)) ×
  has_homsets pgpd.

(** The morphism part of an isomorphism is an inclusion. *)

C: category
a, b: C
isincl (morphism_from_z_iso a b)


C: category
a, b: C
isincl (morphism_from_z_iso a b)

  
C: category
a, b: C
g: C ⟦ a, b ⟧
isofhlevel 1 (hfiber (morphism_from_z_iso a b) g)

  
C: category
a, b: C
g: C ⟦ a, b ⟧
isofhlevel 1 (is_z_isomorphism g)

  apply isaprop_is_z_isomorphism.
Qed.

(** The alternative characterization implies the normal one.
    Note that the other implication is missing, it should be completed
    if possible. *)

pgpd: groupoid
is_univalent_pregroupoid pgpd → is_univalent pgpd


pgpd: groupoid
is_univalent_pregroupoid pgpd → is_univalent pgpd

  
pgpd: groupoid
ig: is_univalent_pregroupoid pgpd
is_univalent pgpd

  
pgpd: groupoid
ig: is_univalent_pregroupoid pgpd
a, b: pgpd
isweq (λ p : a = b, idtoiso p)

  
pgpd: groupoid
ig: is_univalent_pregroupoid pgpd
a, b: pgpd
isofhlevelf 0 (λ x : a = b, idtoiso x)
pgpd: groupoid
ig: is_univalent_pregroupoid pgpd
a, b: pgpd
isofhlevelf 1 (morphism_from_z_iso a b)

  
pgpd: groupoid
ig: is_univalent_pregroupoid pgpd
a, b: pgpd
isofhlevelf 0 (λ x : a = b, idtoiso x)
 
pgpd: groupoid
ig: is_univalent_pregroupoid pgpd
a, b: pgpd
idtomor a b ~ (λ x : a = b, idtoiso x)
pgpd: groupoid
ig: is_univalent_pregroupoid pgpd
a, b: pgpd
isweq (idtomor a b)

    
pgpd: groupoid
ig: is_univalent_pregroupoid pgpd
a, b: pgpd
idtomor a b ~ (λ x : a = b, idtoiso x)
 intro p; destruct p; reflexivity.
    
pgpd: groupoid
ig: is_univalent_pregroupoid pgpd
a, b: pgpd
isweq (idtomor a b)
 apply ig.
  
pgpd: groupoid
ig: is_univalent_pregroupoid pgpd
a, b: pgpd
isofhlevelf 1 (morphism_from_z_iso a b)
 apply (morphism_from_iso_is_incl pgpd).
Qed.

(** ** Lemmas *)

(** In a pregroupoid, the hom-types are equivalent to the type of isomorphisms. *)

pgpd: pregroupoid
a, b: pgpd
pgpd ⟦ a, b ⟧ ≃ z_iso a b


pgpd: pregroupoid
a, b: pgpd
pgpd ⟦ a, b ⟧ ≃ z_iso a b

  
pgpd: pregroupoid
a, b: pgpd
pgpd ⟦ a, b ⟧ → z_iso a b
pgpd: pregroupoid
a, b: pgpd
z_iso a b → pgpd ⟦ a, b ⟧
pgpd: pregroupoid
a, b: pgpd
∏ x : pgpd ⟦ a, b ⟧, ?g (?f x) = x
pgpd: pregroupoid
a, b: pgpd
∏ y : z_iso a b, ?f (?g y) = y

  
pgpd: pregroupoid
a, b: pgpd
pgpd ⟦ a, b ⟧ → z_iso a b
 intros f; refine (f,, _); apply pregroupoid_is_pregroupoid.
  
pgpd: pregroupoid
a, b: pgpd
z_iso a b → pgpd ⟦ a, b ⟧
 apply pr1.
  
pgpd: pregroupoid
a, b: pgpd
∏ x : pgpd ⟦ a, b ⟧,
pr1
  ((λ f : pgpd ⟦ a, b ⟧,
    f,, pregroupoid_is_pregroupoid pgpd a b f) x) = x
 reflexivity.
  
pgpd: pregroupoid
a, b: pgpd
∏ y : z_iso a b,
(λ f : pgpd ⟦ a, b ⟧,
 f,, pregroupoid_is_pregroupoid pgpd a b f) 
  (pr1 y) = y
 intro; apply z_iso_eq; reflexivity.
Defined.


pgpd: pregroupoid
a: pgpd
pregroupoid_hom_weq_iso a a (identity a) =
idtoiso (idpath a)


pgpd: pregroupoid
a: pgpd
pregroupoid_hom_weq_iso a a (identity a) =
idtoiso (idpath a)

  apply z_iso_eq; reflexivity.
Defined.


pgpd: pregroupoid
a, b, c: pgpd
f: pgpd ⟦ a, b ⟧
g: pgpd ⟦ b, c ⟧
z_iso_comp (pregroupoid_hom_weq_iso a b f)
  (pregroupoid_hom_weq_iso b c g) =
pregroupoid_hom_weq_iso a c (f · g)


pgpd: pregroupoid
a, b, c: pgpd
f: pgpd ⟦ a, b ⟧
g: pgpd ⟦ b, c ⟧
z_iso_comp (pregroupoid_hom_weq_iso a b f)
  (pregroupoid_hom_weq_iso b c g) =
pregroupoid_hom_weq_iso a c (f · g)

  apply z_iso_eq; reflexivity.
Defined.

(** If D is a groupoid, then a functor category into it is as well. *)

C: precategory
D: category
gr_D: is_pregroupoid D
is_pregroupoid [C, D]


C: precategory
D: category
gr_D: is_pregroupoid D
is_pregroupoid [C, D]

  
C: precategory
D: category
gr_D: is_pregroupoid D
F, G: [C, D]
α: [C, D] ⟦ F, G ⟧
is_nat_z_iso (pr1 α)

  intros c; apply gr_D.
Defined.

(** In a univalent groupoid, arrows are equivalent to paths *)

ugpd: univalent_groupoid
a, b: ugpd
ugpd ⟦ a, b ⟧ ≃ a = b


ugpd: univalent_groupoid
a, b: ugpd
ugpd ⟦ a, b ⟧ ≃ a = b

  
ugpd: univalent_groupoid
a, b: ugpd
ugpd ⟦ a, b ⟧ ≃ z_iso a b
ugpd: univalent_groupoid
a, b: ugpd
z_iso a b ≃ a = b

  
ugpd: univalent_groupoid
a, b: ugpd
ugpd ⟦ a, b ⟧ ≃ z_iso a b
 apply (@pregroupoid_hom_weq_iso ugpd).
  
ugpd: univalent_groupoid
a, b: ugpd
z_iso a b ≃ a = b
 
ugpd: univalent_groupoid
a, b: ugpd
a = b → z_iso a b
ugpd: univalent_groupoid
a, b: ugpd
isweq ?f

    
ugpd: univalent_groupoid
a, b: ugpd
a = b → z_iso a b
 exact idtoiso.
    
ugpd: univalent_groupoid
a, b: ugpd
isweq idtoiso
 apply univalent_category_is_univalent.
Defined.

                       is_z_isomorphism f)),
                 (C,,
                  (λ a1 b1 : C,
                   ∑ f : C ⟦ a1, b1 ⟧,
                   is_z_isomorphism f)) ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧
                 → (C,,
                    (λ a1 b1 : C,
                     ∑ f : C ⟦ a1, b1 ⟧,
                     is_z_isomorphism f)) ⟦ b0, c ⟧
                   → (C,,
                      (λ a1 b1 : C,
                       ∑ f : C ⟦ a1, b1 ⟧,
                       is_z_isomorphism f)) ⟦ a0, c ⟧))
             :
             (λ C : precategory_ob_mor,
              precategory_id_comp C)
               (C,,
                (λ a0 b0 : C,
                 ∑ f : C ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧,
                 is_z_isomorphism f)))) ⟦ a, b ⟧),
      z_iso_eq (f · identity b) f (id_right f)))

                   (λ a0 : C,
                    identity a0,, identity_is_z_iso a0)
                   (λ (a0 b0 c0 : C)
                    (f0 : ∑ f0 : C ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧,
                          is_z_isomorphism f0)
                    (g : ∑ f1 : C ⟦ b0, c0 ⟧,
                         is_z_isomorphism f1),
                    z_iso_comp f0 g)
                 :
                 (∏
                  c0 : C,,
                       (λ a0 b0 : C,
                        ∑ f0 : C ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧,
                        is_z_isomorphism f0),
                  (C,,
                   (λ a0 b0 : C,
                    ∑ f0 : C ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧,
                    is_z_isomorphism f0)) ⟦ c0, c0 ⟧)
                 × (∏
                    (a0 : C,,
                          (λ a0 b0 : C,
                           ∑ f0 : C ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧,
                           is_z_isomorphism f0))
                    (b0 : C,,
                          (λ a1 b0 : C,
                           ∑ f0 : C ⟦ a1, b0 ⟧,
                           is_z_isomorphism f0))
                    (c0 : C,,
                          (λ a1 b1 : C,
                           ∑ f0 : C ⟦ a1, b1 ⟧,
                           is_z_isomorphism f0)),
                    (C,,
                     (λ a1 b1 : C,
                      ∑ f0 : ..., is_z_isomorphism f0))
                    ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧
                    → (C,, (λ a1 b1 : C, ∑ ..., ...))
                      ⟦ b0, c0 ⟧
                      → (C,, (λ a1 b1 : C, ∑ ..., ...))
                        ⟦ a0, c0 ⟧))
                :
                (λ C : precategory_ob_mor,
                 precategory_id_comp C)
                  (C,,
                   (λ a0 b0 : C,
                    ∑ f0 : C ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧,
                    is_z_isomorphism f0)))) ⟦ b, c ⟧)
         (h : ((C,,
                (λ a0 b0 : C,
                 ∑ f0 : C ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧,
                 is_z_isomorphism f0)),,
               ((make_dirprod
                   (λ a0 : C,
                    identity a0,, identity_is_z_iso a0)
                   (λ (a0 b0 c0 : C)
                    (f0 : ∑ f0 : C ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧,
                          is_z_isomorphism f0)
                    (g0 : ∑ f1 : C ⟦ b0, c0 ⟧,
                          is_z_isomorphism f1),
                    z_iso_comp f0 g0)
                 :
                 (∏
                  c0 : C,,
                       (λ a0 b0 : C,
                        ∑ f0 : C ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧,
                        is_z_isomorphism f0),
                  (C,,
                   (λ a0 b0 : C,
                    ∑ f0 : C ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧,
                    is_z_isomorphism f0)) ⟦ c0, c0 ⟧)
                 × (∏
                    (a0 : C,,
                          (λ a0 b0 : C,
                           ∑ f0 : C ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧,
                           is_z_isomorphism f0))
                    (b0 : C,,
                          (λ a1 b0 : C,
                           ∑ f0 : C ⟦ a1, b0 ⟧,
                           is_z_isomorphism f0))
                    (c0 : C,,
                          (λ a1 b1 : C,
                           ∑ f0 : C ⟦ a1, b1 ⟧,
                           is_z_isomorphism f0)),
                    (C,,
                     (λ a1 b1 : C,
                      ∑ f0 : ..., is_z_isomorphism f0))
                    ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧
                    → (C,, (λ a1 b1 : C, ∑ ..., ...))
                      ⟦ b0, c0 ⟧
                      → (C,, (λ a1 b1 : C, ∑ ..., ...))
                        ⟦ a0, c0 ⟧))
                :
                (λ C : precategory_ob_mor,
                 precategory_id_comp C)
                  (C,,
                   (λ a0 b0 : C,
                    ∑ f0 : C ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧,
                    is_z_isomorphism f0)))) ⟦ c, d ⟧),
         z_iso_eq (f · g · h) (f · (g · h))
           (assoc' f g h))))

has_homsets
  (C,,
   (λ a b : C, ∑ f : C ⟦ a, b ⟧, is_z_isomorphism f))

                         (λ a0 : C,
                          identity a0,,
                          identity_is_z_iso a0)
                         (λ (a0 b0 c0 : C)
                          (f0 : ∑ f0 : ...,
                                is_z_isomorphism f0)
                          (g0 : ∑ f1 : ...,
                                is_z_isomorphism f1),
                          z_iso_comp f0 g0)
                       :
                       (∏ c0 : C,, (...),
                        (C,, ...) ⟦ c0, c0 ⟧)
                       × (∏ (a0 : C,, (...))
                          (b0 : C,, (...))
                          (c0 : C,, (...)),
                          (...) ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧
                          → ... ⟦ b0, c0 ⟧
                            → ... ⟦ a0, c0 ⟧))
                      :
                      (λ C : precategory_ob_mor,
                       precategory_id_comp C)
                        (C,,
                         (λ a0 b0 : C,
                          ∑ f0 : C ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧,
                          is_z_isomorphism f0)))) ⟦ c,
                    d ⟧),
               z_iso_eq (f · g · h) (f · (g · h))
                 (assoc' f g h))))))

          (λ a b : C,
           ∑ f : C ⟦ a, b ⟧, is_z_isomorphism f))

Defined.

(** ** Discrete categories *)

(** See [Categories.Categories.StandardCategories] for a proof that any discrete
    category is equivalent to the path groupoid of its objects. *)

(** A discrete category is a univalent [pregroupoid] with an underlying [setcategory].
    Why? In this case, all arrows must be identities: every arrow has an inverse,
    and isos induce equality (by univalence).
 *)
Definition is_discrete (C : category) :=
  (is_setcategory C × is_pregroupoid C × is_univalent C).

Definition discrete_category : UU := ∑ C : category, is_discrete C.
Definition make_discrete_category :
  ∏ C : category, is_discrete C → discrete_category := tpair is_discrete.
Definition discrete_category_to_univalent_groupoid :
  discrete_category -> univalent_groupoid :=
  λ disc, make_univalent_groupoid
            (make_univalent_category (pr1 disc) (dirprod_pr2 (dirprod_pr2 (pr2 disc))))
            (dirprod_pr1 (dirprod_pr2 (pr2 disc))).
Coercion discrete_category_to_univalent_groupoid :
  discrete_category >-> univalent_groupoid.
Definition discrete_category_is_discrete :
  ∏ C : discrete_category, is_discrete C := pr2.
Definition discrete_category_is_setcategory :
  ∏ C : discrete_category, is_setcategory C := λ C, dirprod_pr1 (pr2 C).


C: category
isaprop (is_discrete C)


C: category
isaprop (is_discrete C)

  
C: category
isaprop (is_setcategory C)
C: category
isaprop (is_pregroupoid C)
C: category
isaprop (is_univalent C)

  
C: category
isaprop (is_setcategory C)
 apply isaprop_is_setcategory.
  
C: category
isaprop (is_pregroupoid C)
 apply isaprop_is_pregroupoid.
  
C: category
isaprop (is_univalent C)
 apply isaprop_is_univalent.
Defined.
